      <div class="container">
       <div class="content-slot-container hidden-xs" id="slot-footer-company-description">
        <div class="footer-company-description" id="footer-company-description">
         <!-- dwMarker="content" dwContentID="bcXagiaaie7ecaaadenEJNlFW0" -->
         <div class="content-asset" id="printable">
          <!-- dwMarker="content" dwContentID="bcXagiaaie7ecaaadenEJNlFW0" -->
          <p class="footerText">
           <strong>
            PUMA at a Glance
           </strong>
           / PUMA is one of the worlds leading sports brands, designing, developing, selling, and marketing footwear, apparel, and accessories. For over 65 years, PUMA has established a history of making fast product designs for the fastest athletes on the planet. PUMA offers performance and sport-inspired lifestyle products in categories such as
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/sports/soccer">
            Football
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/sports/running">
            Running
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/sports/training">
            Training
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/sports/golf">
            Golf
           </a>
           , and
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/men/sport/motorsport">
            Motorsport
           </a>
           . It engages in exciting collaborations with renowned design brands such as Alexander McQueen and Mihara Yasuhiro to bring innovative and fast designs to the sports world.
          </p>
          <p>
           The official PUMA Online Store offers a large selection of PUMA shoes, clothing, accessories, and equipment.
          </p>
          <p>
           PUMAs family of star players in football includes Sergio Agero, Cesc Fbregas, Marco Reus, Radamel Falcao, Olivier Giroud,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/ambassadors/mario-balotelli">
            Mario Balotelli
           </a>
           , and, in womens football, Brazilian powerhouse Marta. PUMA also sponsors a number of influential national and club teams, including four-time world champion
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/teams/italia">
            Italy
           </a>
           , Austria, Switzerland, Uruguay, Chile, Ghana, Ivory Coast, and Cameroon, plus
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/teams/bvb">
            Borussia Dortmund
           </a>
           , Newcastle United FC, and
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/teams/arsenal">
            Arsenal FC
           </a>
           (from July 2014). The PUMA Running collection, notable for innovative new product like our Faas and Mobium shoes, is represented by the fastest man in the world, sprinter
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/ambassadors/usain-bolt">
            Usain Bolt
           </a>
           . (Nuff said.)
          </p>
          <p>
           In Golf, such game-changing athletes as
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/ambassadors/rickie-fowler">
            Rickie Fowler
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/sports/ambassadors/lexi-thompson">
            Lexi Thompson
           </a>
           , Graham DeLaet, Greg Norman, and Will MacKenzie represent COBRA PUMA GOLF.
          </p>
          <p>
           PUMAs sport-inspired lifestyle products include the
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/men/sport/motorsport">
            PUMA Motorsport collection
           </a>
           , which features officially licensed gear from Ferrari, BMW Motorsport, and Mercedes AMG Petronas.
          </p>
          <p>
           PUMA has created famous sneaker styles such as the
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/pd/suede-classic-%2B-mens-sneakers/pna352634.html">
            Suede
           </a>
           , El Rey,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/pd/roma-mens-sneakers/pna353572.html">
            Roma
           </a>
           , Clyde,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/pd/mostro-perf-leather-shoes/pna351413.html">
            Mostro
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/pd/speed-cat-sd-shoes/pna301953.html">
            Speed Cat
           </a>
           , Basket, Disc Blaze,
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/pd/gv-special/pna343569.html">
            GV Special
           </a>
           , and Trinomic range  as well as icons-to-be like our Sport Lite styles and, for women, our
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/women/footwear/sneakers/wedge">
            sneaker wedges
           </a>
           and
           <a href="http://us.puma.com/en_US/women/shoes/ballerinas">
            ballet flats
           </a>
           . Creative partnerships with influential brand advocates like Meek Mill, Solange, and Bucky Lasek round out our lifestyle category.
          </p>
          <p>
           The company distributes its products in more than 120 countries, employs more than 10,000 people worldwide, and is headquartered in Herzogenaurach, Germany.
          </p>
         </div>
         <!-- End content-asset -->
